				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Christ lag in Todes Banden, BWV 4 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 movements
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1707 in Arnstadt (for Mühlhausen)<br />1724-25 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>

<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">Christ lag in Todes Banden&#160;; Christ lag in Todesbanden
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Christ lay in Death's Bonds
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Bach,_Johann_Sebastian" title="Category:Bach, Johann Sebastian">Bach, Johann Sebastian</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Opus/Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">Op./Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>BWV 4&#160;; BC A 54a-b
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IJB 736
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Key
</th>
<td>E minor
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>8 movements:
<ol><li>Sinfonia
</li><li>Chorus: Christ lag in Todes Banden
</li><li>Duetto (soprano, alto): Den Tod niemand zwingen kunnt
</li><li>Aria (tenor): Jesus Christus, Gottes Sohn
</li><li>Chorus: Es war ein wunderlicher Krieg
</li><li>Aria (bass): Hier ist das rechte Osterlamm
</li><li>Duetto Aria (soprano, tenor): So feiern wir das hohe Fest
</li><li>Chorale: Wir essen und leben wohl
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Year/Date of Composition</span><span class="ms555">Y/D of Comp.</span>
</th>
<td>1707 in Arnstadt (for Mühlhausen)<br />1724-25 in Leipzig
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1707-04-24 in Mühlhausen (1st Performance, trial performance for post of Organist at Divi Blasii [No. 8 uses music from No. 2])<br />1708-04-08 in Mühlhausen (2nd Performance [No. 8 uses music from No. 2])<br />1724-04-09 in Leipzig (3rd Performance)<br />1725-04-01 in Leipzig (4th Performance [included brass instruments in this version])
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1851 (BGA)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Luther,_Martin" title="Category:Luther, Martin">Martin Luther</a> (1483–1546)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Language
</th>
<td>German
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Dedication
</th>
<td>Easter Sunday
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Average Duration</span><span class="ms555">Avg. Duration</span>
</th>
<td>20 minutes
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque" title="Category:Baroque">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Baroque_style" title="Category:Baroque style">Baroque</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td><i>Voices:</i> soprano, alto, tenor, bass; mixed chorus (SATB)<br /><i>Orchestra:</i> cornetto (3rd version), 3 trombones (3rd version), strings (2 violas), continuo
</td></tr>
<tr>
